(роЗ) роЗ#рпЗро▒, роП#? asked the Prime Minister and Minister of National Policies and Economic Affairs:

(a) Will he inform this House -

(i) the number of horses available in the mounted horse units of the three armed forces of Army, Air Force and Navy;

(роЗ) роЗ#рпЗро▒, роП#?

asked the Minister of Irrigation and Water Resources Management:

(a) Will he inform this House in relation to the Puttalam District by the year 1983 -

(i) the number of irrigation systems that had existed;

(ii) the number of small-scale tanks, anicuts and canals that had existed; and

(iii) the extent of lands that had been brought under cultivation?

(b) Will he also inform this House -

(i) separately on per year basis from year 1983 until the war situation had ended in 2009 the amount of money that had been allocated for restoration of irrigation schemes, tanks, anicuts and canals; and

(ii) separately on per year basis from the time the war situation ended until year 2015 the total amount of money the government had allocated for the restoration of irrigation systems, tanks, anicuts and canals?

(c) If not, why? р╢Ь. р╢Ьр╖ПOv Iw< Iр╢вр╢║qx р╖Щр╖ГGlр╖Гр╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (р╖Ар╖П=р╢╕р╖Пр╢Ь р╖Др╖П р╢вр╢╜р╖Гр╢┤< р╢Ър╖Ер╢╕р╢▒р╖Пр╢Ър╢╗р╢л р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нe-р╢╕р╖П) (рооро╛ рооро┐ роХро╛рооро┐ройро┐ ро╡ро┐роЬро┐' ро╡ро┐роЬроп ройро┐ рпЖроЪро╛>роЪро╛ - роирпА.рокро╛роЪрой роо+, роирпАро░роХ ро╡ро│@ро▓ роХро╛рпИроо'ро╡ роЕрпИроо/роЪ) (The Hon. (роЖ) роЗ#рпЗро▒, роП#?

asked the Minister of Fisheries and Aquatic Resources Development: (a) Will he inform this House - (i) whether there is a housing scheme for Sri Lankan fishermen with the assistance of the Korean National Fisheries Solidarity Federation; (ii) whether that housing scheme is implemented throughout the Island; (iii) whether houses would be constructed for the fishermen in the Northern and Eastern Provinces of the country, who were severely affected by the war as well as natural disasters, under this scheme; (iv) if so, the number of houses that would be constructed, the areas and the dates of construction?

asked the Minister of Lands and Parliamentary Reforms:

(a) Will he inform this House, -

(i) whether the 370 acre land which belongs to the Land Reform Commission, situated in

2017 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& 21

Punnakuda Village in Eravur area in Chenkallady Divisional Secretary's Division in Batticaloa District has been kept for a long period of time without being utilized for any development activity, any construction work or as an unoccupied land;

(ii) whether this land has been identified with the knowledge of the Divisional Secretary to set up an industrial zone;

(iii) Accordingly, whether a request has been made from the Land Reform Commission to legally convey this land to the Board of Investment of Sri Lanka to establish an Industrial Zone;

(iv) whether the Board of Investment of Sri Lanka has assigned to Lanka Hydraulic Institution the task of conducting the preliminary study requires to establish an investment zone in the aforesaid land, at a cost of 38 million rupees;

(vi) the reason for not taking action by the relevant authorities to remove the unauthorized constructions?

(роЗ) роЗ#рпЗро▒ роП#? asked the Minister of Health, Nutrition and Indigenous Medicine:

(a) Is he aware that-

(i) the Divisional hospitals at Mankerni, Mahiloor, Mancholai, Unnichchai, Kathiraveli, Mandur and Mahilawattawan in Batticaloa District are temporarily closed for want of Medical Officers;

(ii) the buildings exist with other facilities and name boards;

(iii) patients in these areas undergo immense hardships while travelling to far away places for medical treatment as a result of poor transport facilities; and

(iv) the concept of providing free medical services for the poor village patients is not fulfilled?

(b) Will he inform this House-

(i) whether action will be taken to reopen these Hospitals and to provide at least two medical officers; and

(ii) the date that these hospitals will be reopened to function?

(c) If not, why?

(iii) if so, of the date on which it was done;

(iv) the number of permanent, temporary and probationary lecturers in that Department; and

(v) the recruitment procedure adopted for temporary/probationary lecturers?

(роЖ) роЗ#рпЗро▒, роП#? asked the Minister of Public Administration and Management: (a) Will he inform this House-

(i) whether promotions have been given contravening the approval of the Public Services Commission with relevance to the promotion of officers to the special grade as per the Sri Lanka Accountants' Service Minutes published by Gazette Extraordinary No.1670/33 dated 10.09.2010;

(ii) whether a request has been made by the Secretary to the Ministry of Finance regarding the provision of special grade promotions to officers without post graduate qualifications;

(iii) if so, the aforesaid period;

(iv) whether the Public Services Commission has granted the approval required;

р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А

(v) whether 82 officers have been called for the said interview;

(vi) whether a register including the names of officers who belonged to the particular period approved by the Public Services Commission, and another including the names of those who do not belong to the particular period, will be submitted;

(vii) whether these officers have been promoted to the special grade;

(viii) if so, the effective date of the said promotions;

(ix) the officers who should be held responsible if promotions have been given contravening the regulations stipulated by the Public Services Commission;

(x) the steps that will be taken regarding these officers;

(xi) the steps that will be taken on behalf of the officers who were subjected to injustice due to not been promoted?

(b) If not, why?

Tilak Marapana -Minister of Development Assignments and Minister of Foreign Affairs) Hon. Speaker, in regard to the Question raised by the Hon. Dinesh Gunawardena under Standing Order No. 23 (2) on 06th September, 2017, I would like to mention that there is a complaint that has been lodged in the Public ProsecutorтАЩs Office in Brazil by a Non-governmental Organization requesting the Brazilian Authorities to take legal action against General Jagath Jayasuriya on alleged war crimes that he is supposed to have committed. We have only received an unofficial translation of the papers that have been filed in the Brazilian office.

I have also been informed that earlier also on two previous occasions - in 2011 in the United States of America, and again in September, 2011 in Switzerland - similar complaints were lodged by NGOs in other countries against members of the armed forces. So, this is not a new thing. Those legal actions filed earlier were dismissed by the respective countries.

In regard to the second question raised by the Hon. Member on the material that has been filed against General Jagath Jayasuriya in Brazil, there is no credible evidence presented that General Jayasuriya was in anyway engaged in any illegal actions as alleged against

433 434

[р╢ЬL р╢Ср╖Гр╖К.┬╗. р╖Гр╖Пр╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П]

2017 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& 21

him. So, I think in that situation, the question of his being prosecuted or the question of our having to defend him in any of those proceedings will not arise. Furthermore, these complaints were made only after General Jagath JayasuriyaтАЩs term was over and actually, he had left Brazil at the time these complaints were lodged in the Public ProsecutorтАЩs Office. Therefore, it does not seem that this is a bona fide complaint.

As regards the third question the Hon. Member raised, I wish to say that Field Marshal Sarath FonsekaтАЩs statements only set out his personal views on this issue. The official version has been well articulated by His Excellency the President which reflects the Government policy on this matter. р╢Ь. bр╖Щр╖Вр╖К nр╢лр╖Ар╢░р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ родро┐рпЗройK рогро╡родрой) (The Hon. Dinesh Gunawardena) Hon. Minister, I want to know whether there have been similar incidents in Colombia or in any other country. р╢Ь. р╢╜" р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╢┤р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ родро┐ро▓ рооро╛ро░рокрой) (The Hon. Tilak Marapana) I have mentioned in my answer, Hon. Member, that on two previous occasions also - in 2011 in the United States of America and again in September, 2011 in Switzerland - similar complaints had been lodged by NGOs against members of the armed forces. Gamini Jayawickrama Perera) Hon. Deputy Chairman of Committees, I would like to make some comments here. Hon. Member, why do you not put forward your problems in writing so that we can submit it to the Prime Minister and the Government? These are small issues.

There is another matter. You know very well that we are trying to implement so many development projects in the Northern and the Eastern Provinces. But, we need your support. We are trying to discuss with the Provincial Councils, Members of Parliament and local government bodies to work out a plan. So, my Ministry is ready for that. I am the one who met the Chief Minister regarding

this. I have known him since 1977. Then, he was a judge. We will give you our co-operation. Hon. Member had been working with us and we went even to the Kachcheri. So, please, submit us any problem in writing. I am ready to attend to it as the Minister of Sustainable Development and Wildlife. It is our duty. Do not call yourselves "Northerners" or "Southerners". We all are Sri Lankans. As you have supported us yesterday to pass the Provincial Councils Elections (Amendment) Bill, we will work together. р╢Ь. р╢Ср╖Гр╖К. Gamini Jayawickrama Perera) I will give you a date. But, I need your support. We have released Rs. 5 million to develop a sustainable village there with a botanical garden, zoological garden and crop cultivation which are suitable to that area. Yet, we are unable to get the support we need. We have contacted the Chief Minister and met with the Chief Secretary. I told the Chief Minister about this matter. Your colleague Provincial Council Ministers and Members know the matter, but we are unable to get their support. So, support us.

We have allocated money for the development of the Delft Island and we are doing some development work there. I will definitely come. But, we need your support. So, tell the Chief Minister to not to object to it. Then, we will do the development. My problem is that. Some other Ministries also have the same problem. Without being suspicious, the Chief Minister, the Provincial Council and the local authorities have to help us. We, the Ministries, want to develop the infrastructure in your area. р╢Ь. р╢Ср╖Гр╖К. р╢Ь. р╢Ьр╖ПOv р╢вр╢║I┬Ар╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щр╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ роХро╛рооро┐ройро┐ роЬропро╡ро┐ро░роо рпЖрокрпЗро░ро░ро╛) (The Hon. Gamini Jayawickrama Perera) I think, I replied to it in a statement saying that all the Ministries should go in line with the sustainable development programme. I agree with you. My Ministry alone cannot do it. So, I am proposing that all the Ministries have to do their part of the work. The main part has to be done by the Ministries which come under the Central Government, the Provincial Councils and then the local bodies. So, we have to interlink.

I think the rehabilitation of Iranamadu Tank comes under the Irrigation Department in the Provincial Council. So, in that way, tank development work comes under the Irrigation Departments coming under the Provincial Councils. So, those have to be linked. Providing Central Government funds is not a problem. That can be provided. Therefore, we will work together. I will point out what you said at the next Cabinet Meeting. р╢Ь. р╢Ср╖Гр╖К. р╢Ь. р╢╗~р╖Жр╖К р╖Д┬д р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (р╢▒р╢Ьр╢╗ р╖Гр╖Рр╢╜ р╖Др╖П р╢вр╢╜ р╖Гр╢┤р╖Пр╢пр╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нe-р╢╕р╖П) (рооро╛ рооро┐ ро▒T. ро╣роХрпА - роироХро░' родро┐1роЯрооро┐роЯ8 роо+, роирпА ро╡ро┤0роХ8 роЕрпИроо/роЪ) (The Hon. Rauff Hakeem - Minister of City Planning and Water Supply) Bismillahir Rahmanir Raheem.

Hon. Deputy Chairman of Committees, we are discussing, matters relating to sustainable development in this country. I must, at the outset, congratulate my

469 470

[р╢ЬL р╢Ср╖Гр╖К. tр╢нр╢╗' р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П]

2017 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& 21

Colleague, the Hon. Minister, Gamini Jayawickrama Perera, who is one of the senior-most Members in this House, among the very few people who have been in the 1977 Parliament along with the Hon. Prime Minister.

So, we are all fortunate to be working along with a very senior, experienced and a humble politician - a man of the people. He has, in fact, been given the responsibility of being in charge of this particular Ministry that has been exclusively created to look after our countryтАЩs efforts towards reaching the Sustainable Development Goals set up by the United Nations.

As we know, the Sustainable Development Goals' initiative is a continuation of the Millennium Development Goals' initiative that expired in 2015. Now we have the next one-and-a-half decades to achieve the 2030 target and 17 such goals have been identified. So, we can speak at length of all the goals. These goals will help the people achieve prosperity in our planet and it seeks to strengthen the universal peace through eradication of poverty, reversing climate change and achieving gender equality. I believe these are all very laudable objectives and particularly, to achieve prosperity and to eradicate poverty, much has to be done. We know several governments initiated programmes previously known as тАШJana Saviya SchemeтАЩ by the Premadasa Regime and now called the тАШSamurdhi SchemeтАЩ by our Government. All of which go to support the underprivileged families who have a massive income gap to manage. In our poverty alleviation schemes, it is important for us to have a sustainable development programme aiming to bring these people out of the callous and deliberately uncaring situation to which they have all been subjected.

The collaborative partnership between the people and the Government to implement these objectives is the most important aspect of the Hon. MinisterтАЩs work. The policymakers have to map out strategies to overcome challenges to make sure the planet is secure for succeeding generations to enjoy its bounties.

I must remind here, that this Parliament has set up a special Select Committee on the United Nations 2030 Agenda for Sustainable Development, which is also a laudable initiative and our Hon. Deputy Speaker is chairing that Select Committee. That Select Committee is empowered to monitor, support and also make this House aware of the need to keep the focus on the Sustainable Development Goals.

Growth must be both inclusive and environmentally sound to reduce poverty and to build shared prosperity. In that regard, I believe we have to deliver immediate long-term benefits for people as well as to the entire planet to ensure prosperity of the people. р╢Ь. р╢Ьр╖ПOv р╢вр╢║I┬Ар╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щр╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ роХро╛рооро┐ройро┐ роЬропро╡ро┐ро░роо рпЖрокрпЗро░ро░ро╛) (The Hon. Gamini Jayawickrama Perera) р╢▒р╖Р┬е J┬Кр╖ЩLр╢║. роО63родро╛. rose.

Tр╢║5р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖П р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢Ър╢╗р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╖Б?р╢║, р╢╢┬Ш р╢вр╖П?р╢ЪMр╖Ар╢║, р╢╢┬Ш р╢Жр╢Ь7р╢ЪMр╖Ар╢║ р╢Фр╖Гр╖Кр╖Щр╖Гn р╖Щ. р╢╗р╢з р╢ЙXр╢║р╢з р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╢║'р╢▒ р╢Ер╢нр╖Ар╖БU. р╢Т р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM u р╢║р╖Ар╢╗ р╢║р╢з р╢нр╢╕U р╢Ер╢п р╢Лр╢пр╖Ср╖Гр╢▒ р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╖Щр╢Ъ^.р╢┤р╢н р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Щр╖Еn. р╢С2 р╢║. р╢Еa р╢┤р╖Пaр╖А р╢п"р╢▒р╖Ар╖П р╢▒., р╢Е р╖Пр╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖П %р╢Ър╖Пр╖Б р╢Ър╖Е р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢║р╢з, р╢Т р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢▒ vр╢┤р╢║р╢╕ р╖Щр╖А' р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П, р╢Т р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Ар╖Пр╢п р╖Ар╖Пр╢п р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П, р╖Щ р╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╖Щр╢Ър╢лр╖Щр╢║' р╢╢р╢╜'р╖Щ' р╢▒р╖Р?р╖А р╢Т р╖Щ р╖А! ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖П р╢н р╖А'р╖Щ' р╢Е?р╢ЬL р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢┤? р╢╕р╖П р╢║р╢зр╖ЩMU. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│ ┬др╢║р╖Пр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ. р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ыр╖Пр╖А ?р╢╗р╖Гр╖Пр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖П р╢║р╢зр╖ЩM ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢нр╢▒ р╢╗ р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖Пр╢з р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╕ р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ ┬б┬╡┬б р╖Щр╢Ър╢▒р╖Пр╢з ┬б┬╡┬б р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╢║ 0р╢╕ "р╢║р╢╜р╖ПU р╢╕р╖П р╖Бр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╖Г р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ'. р╢Кр╢з р╖Щр╖Дn р╖А р╖Щ.р╢ЪU. р╢С р╢╕р╖П %р╢░р╖Пр╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╢║р╢з р╢Ер╖Щ= р╖Ар╢║р╢╣ р╢┤р╖Ер╖Пр╢нр╢з р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ v&?р╢║ р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ ┬╡' р╖Щр╢Ър╖Щр╢▒.

р╢Т р╢нр╢╗ р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╖АU. р╢С р╢╕р╖П р╖Ар╢║р╢╣ р╢┤р╖Ер╖Пр╖ЩM р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ ┬Ч0р╢╕ р╢З? р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢┤р╖Рр╖Др╖РDр╖А "Hр╖Щр╖А1M, р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢ЬL р╢Й'р╢Ъ р╢ЕVL р╢░ р╖Щр╖Дnр╢╗M р╢╕'S р╢╕р╖П "Hр╖Ар╖П р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$ р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╖Др╖ПN р╖Щр╢▒1р╢Ър╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ T┬╡ р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1 р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п "р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢Ф= р╢Ър╢╗ р╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ър╖Щр╢║ р╢нр╢╕U, р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖П. р╖Щр╢╕1р╢Ър╢п, р╢С р╢╕р╖Пр╖Щ$ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜ р╖Ар╢Ър╖Ар╖ПVр╖А р╖Е р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╢зр╖Гр╖К р╢Ьр╢лр╢▒р╖Пр╖А р╢Й^ р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢┤р╖РMр╢н"' р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢Ьр╖Щр╢▒р╢▒ р╢Ьр╢╕' р╢Ьр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Е р╖Гр╢нр╖П ┬╖р╢┤р╖Пр╖Ар╖П р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖П р╢Ър╢╗р╢Ь'р╢▒, р╢ЕD р╢Ьр╖Др╢▒р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢З? u р╢нMMр╖Ар╢║'р╢з р╢║. р╖Г├Ър╢╕ р╖Щр╢п'р╢▒, р╖Ар╢▒р╖П'р╢нр╢╗ р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖П р╢Ър╢╗р╢Ь'р╢▒, р╢Т Tр╢║!р╢╜ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖Ар╢║р╢╣ р╢┤р╖Ер╖Пр╖ЩM р╢╕р╖Д р╢Зр╢╕?р╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╢║р╢з р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╢╕р╖Д'Tр╢║ р╢пр╢╗ , р╢Ър╖Рр╢┤Jр╢╕ р╢Ър╢╗ р╖Щр╢Ър╖Щр╢▒, р╢С р╢╕р╖П. р╢Т р╢нр╢╗. р╖Щр╢пр╢║ р╢Ър╢╗ р╢С р╢╕р╖Пр╢з ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║ р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ 0р╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Е?р╢ЬL р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢┤? р╢╕р╖Пр╢зM, р╢ЬL р╢Е р╖Пр╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖Пр╢зM р╢╕р╢╕ р╢┤р╖Еgр╖Щр╖А'р╢╕ р╖Гр╖К ?р╖А'р╢н р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ р╖Гр╢Вр╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ T' 2030 р╖Ар╢▒р╢з ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ "#р╢╕р╢з р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╢╗1M р╖Ар╢▒ ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ "#р╢╕ р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' р╢┤р╖Еgр╖Ар╖РN р╖Ар╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢Фр╢╢ р╢╕р╖П T' р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢┤M р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢┤р╖Еgр╖Ар╖РN р╖Ар╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢Т р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖Пр╖ЩH. р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ "Tр╢╕ р╢╗р╢зр╢Ъ р╢Ср╖Ар╖РN р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢Т р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ р╢С2 р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╢┤? ┬Эр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╢╕р╖П р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗ 0р╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢╕р╖П р╢Е?р╖Бр╢║ р╖Г'р╖Щр╢нр╖В р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖А р╢╕р╢з р╢╜р╖Рzp р╢╕р╖Д р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖А "р╢║р╖П р╢╕р╖П 2р╢нр╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖П р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖П р╢┤MJр╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢Е р╖Г'р╖Щр╢нр╖В р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Е ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║ 2^р╖Ар╢╜р╖П р╢С2 р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ ┬Эр╢╗ р╢Ъ&р╢нр╖А р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖Пр╢з р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ ┬╡'р╢▒р╖П. р╢С р╢╕р╖П р╢┤р╖Рр╖Др╖РDр╖Ар╢╕ р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╖Щр╖Д1┬╜' р╢Т р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╢╗р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╢║р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢╕20 р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╖А&р╢нр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒ р╢нMMр╖Ар╢║ р╖Щр╢╕1р╢Ър╢п "р╢║р╖П р╢╢р╢╜'р╢▒ 7V. р╢п р╢Ер╢нр╖Ар╖БU. р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╢Ъ7^р╖А р╢║р╢з р╢Е р╖Щ. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╢Ър╢з Mр╖ЩM р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬMр╢Ър╢╕ р╢ЪD'р╢╕ р╖Д├Ър╢▒р╖П р╢ЬM р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з, р╢Т р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А р╖Е р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╢╕M р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╖Гр╢зр╖Др╢▒ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢Ъ`р╢йр╖Пр╢║р╢╕ р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Хр╢▒р╖Ср╢╕ р╢╗р╢з"' р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╢зр╢з р╢║. "T р╢Жр╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢║ р╢Ь'р╢▒, р╢Ср╖Щр╖Др╢╕ р╢▒р╖РMр╢▒. р╢лр╢║ р╢Ь'р╢▒ р╖Др╖Р"р╢║р╖Пр╖А р╢╜р╖Рр╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢╗р╖Щx р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Е р╢ЙXр╢┤M "#р╖Щ.0 ┬вDр╢Ъ T р╢░р╖П'р╢н р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з р╢╢р╢╜р╢▒ р╖Щ р╖А! р╢нр╢╕U р╢╕р╖Пр╢▒р╖А р╢ЕU?р╖Ар╖ПTр╢Ъ., р╢╗р╖Щx \?р╢║ ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╖Ар╢▒ р╢║, р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Щр╢║1р╢пр╢▒ %р╖П$р╢░р╢▒ р╢║р╢п., cр╖Вр╢лр╢║"', р╢▒р╖Пр╖Гр╖К?р╢║"' р╖Щр╢н1р╢╗р╖А р╢╗р╖Щx ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╖Ар╢▒ ┬др╢║р╖Пр╢пр╖Пр╢╕р╢║', р╢Т р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ ┬╕р╢╕ р╢пр╖Пр╢║р╢ЪMр╖Ар╢║, р╢Т ┬╕р╢╕ р╢пр╖Пр╢║р╢ЪMр╖Ар╢║р╢з р╢пр╖РVр╢╕ ! "#р╖Щ., ┬Шpр╖А р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╖Щ., N р╢лMр╖Ар╢║ %р╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ "#р╖Щ. р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Д' р╢║р╢▒р╖Пр╢║.

р╢Ср╖Ар╖РN р╖Щр╢пр╢║ "#р╖Щ.0 р╢Т р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒  р╖Др╢║ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╢┤р╖Рр╖Др╖РD р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Др╢▒, 7V. р╢п`р╢й р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢▒р╖РMр╢▒., р╢Е р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Дnр╢п р╢Й'р╖Щ', р╢Е р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Дnр╢зр╢п р╢║'р╖Щ' "р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╖Д├Ър╢▒р╖П р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕р╢з р╢╢р╖РX р╢▒.,  p р╖Щр╖А'р╢▒ 2р╢нр╢▒,  p р╢вр╖П?р╢║ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤M р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П р╢ЙXр╢║р╢з р╢║'р╢▒ р╢ЛMр╖Гр╖Пр╖Д р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╗р╢з р╖Щр╢╜р╖Г р╢вр╖Пр╢н'р╢нр╢╗р╢║ р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╢з р╖Щр╢пр╖Г р╢╢р╢╜'р╖Щ' р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р.

р╖Щ. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╖Щ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╢Й^р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕р╢з р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ср╢╕ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╖Г.├А&р╢л р╖Б?р╢║ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╜р╖П, р╖Щ р╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒р╖Щр╢║' р╖Щр╢н1р╢╗ р╖Ар╖ШM?р╢Ър╢║' р╢Тр╢Ър╢з р╖Щр╢║1g р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П, р╢Т р╢Ер╢║р╢з р╢Ер╖Ар╖Б р╖Щ р╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢ЪMр╖Ар╢║ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╜р╖П р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH р╢Ъ&р╢нр╖А р╢ЙXр╢║р╢з р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╢║р╖Ср╢╕ р╢нр╢╕U р╢Ер╖Щр╢┤' р╢║ Mр╖ЩM.

р╢ЬL р╢Ър╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕N, р╢╕р╢╕ р╢▒р╖Рр╖Ар╢н р╖Ар╢╗ р╢Фр╢╢ р╢╕р╖Пр╢з р╖Гр╖К ? р╖А'р╢н р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П, р╢╕р╢з р╢Ър╢ор╖П "#р╢╕р╢з р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖А р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒. р╢Т р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕, ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ 2030 р╢▒р╖Пр╢║ р╢┤├Яр╢║р╢з р╢ЕVр╖А р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П, р╢С2 р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╢┤? ┬Эр╢╗р╢║ р╢╕р╢з р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒M р╢╕р╖П р╖Гр╖К ? р╖А'р╢н р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з р╢Е р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╢╗р╖П р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║' р╖Щр╢Ь┬Юр╢╗р╖Ар╢║р╢з р╢┤р╖П├Я р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т р╖Щр╢Ь┬Юр╢╗р╖Ар╢║ р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH T┬Вр╢▒ р╢Е 225р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╢зр╢╕ р╢╜р╖Рр╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╖Щ. р╢Ъ&р╢нр╖Ар╢║р╢з р╢Ер╢┤р╖Щ$ р╖Г.├А&р╢л р╖Б?р╢║, р╖Гр╖Др╖Щр╢║р╢Ьр╢║ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢║ U.

р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╖Щр╢▒1р╖А р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢┤р╢╗.р╢┤р╢╗р╖П р╢Ьр╢лр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢пLр╖А'р╖Щ$ р╢Ер╢▒р╖Пр╢Ьр╢нр╢║ р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' ┬кр╢╕р╖АM, р╢╕M р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Др╢▒ р╢Ър╢╗р╖П р╢║р╢▒ р╢╗р╢з р╖Др╖Р┬Вр╢║р╢з р╢ЙXр╢║р╢з р╢║'р╢▒ р╢▒., ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ - sustainable development - р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Щр╢┤р╖Е р╢Ьр╖Р┬бp р╢╗р╢з, р╢Т р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А'

┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╖Ар╢▒ р╢╗р╢з р╢╢р╖А р╢нр╖Д┬ЯL "#р╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Щр╢╕р╢║р╢з Tр╢║5р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖П р╖Г.├А&р╢л р╖Гр╖Др╖Щр╢║р╢Ьр╢║ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢║ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

Jayasena - Deputy Minister of Sustainable Development and Wildlife) gр╢╜┬бр╢▒ р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╢р╖Ар╢▒ р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╢Ер╢п р╢▒р╖Щ t р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖Пр╖А р╖Е ?р╢╗р╖Гр╖Пр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│ р╢вр╖П?р╢Ъ %?р╢┤M?р╢║ р╖Др╖П р╢Лр╢┤р╖Пр╢║ р╢╕р╖П&р╢Ьр╢║ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ "#р╢╕ р╖Гр╖Д ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ "#р╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢п; ?р╢╗р╖Гр╖Пр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А 2^Jр╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢п р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╢┤р╢▒M р╖Щр╢Ъ^.р╢┤р╢н р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░р╖Щр╢║' р╢Ер╢п р╢Лр╖Щ Tр╢з р╖Щ. р╖Ар╢▒ Lр╢╕ р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕'р╢╜р╖П, р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕'р╢╜р╖П р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╖Щр╢пр╖Щр╢▒s р╢ЪLp р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Ер╖П; р╢Ер╢пр╖Др╖Гр╖К р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢С20 р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Гр╖П&р╢ор╢Ъ р╖Щр╖Д1р╢│ р╢Ер╢пр╖Др╖Гр╖К р╖Др╖Рр╖Щр╢╕р╖Щр╢Ь'р╢╕ р╢ЙXр╢┤M ┬Яр╢лр╖П. р╢┤р╖В р╢┤р╖В р╖Щ р╢пр╢║"' р╖Щр╢н1р╢╗р╖А р╢Т Tр╢║5р╢╕ р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕'р╢╜р╖П р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Е р╢ЪLp р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢ЬL р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖ПM, р╢╕р╢╕M р╖Гр╖Рр╢╜"!р╢╜р╢з р╢Ь'р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т р╢ЕVр╖А р╢Ер╢п р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖ЩH 0 р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║' р╢ЪLp vр╢┤р╢║ р╢ЙXр╢┤M "#р╢╕р╢з р╢╕р╖П р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╢╗1M р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╖Др╖П р╖Ар╢▒┬╣ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖П р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║' р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖Пр╢з р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║ р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ 0р╢╕р╢з р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Е?р╢ЬL р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢┤? 2030 р╖А&р╖Вр╖Щ0 ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ р╖Гр╢Вр╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╢╕├Ч' р╢Ф┬Я'р╖Щ$ р╢▒р╖Пр╢║ р╢┤├Яр╢║р╢з р╢ЕVр╖А р╢Ь'р╢▒р╖П р╢╜р╢п ├Вр╢╗р╢л р╢ЕVр╖А t р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖П р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╖Д р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╖Д р╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ъ р╖Г.р╢┤M Eр╢╢р╢│ р╢Жр╢Вfр╢Ъ р╢Еdр╖Вр╢л р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢ЬL р╢Ър╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕р╖П T' р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ер╢пр╖Пр╖Е р╢Ъ7^р╖Щр╖А' р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╢зр╢╕M р╢Е L р╖Ар╖П&р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ьр╢н р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ср╢╕ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖ЩH р╢ЬL р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╢┤? р╖Ар╢▒ ┬йр╢з р╖Щр╢┤р╢╗ р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Е р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH Nр╖Щр╢║р╢в р╢Ър╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ъ р╢╕р╖П р╖Ар╢▒ ?р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ь ┬бр╢╕?р╢┤р╖Пр╢╜ р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖П T' р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ р╢Е L р╖Ар╖П&р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢пр╖Рр╢▒р╢зр╢╕M р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖Ар╢з р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Гр╖Пр╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢л р╖Гр╖Д ?р╖Гр╖Др╢Ьр╢н р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╢Ер╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒Mр╖Ар╢║ ┬╡I┬║р╢╕, р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢в р╖Гр╖Пр╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢лMр╖Ар╢║ р╖Гр╖Д р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖Пр╖А, р╢вр╖П? р╖Щ р╢пр╢║"' р╖Щр╢н1р╢╗р╖А Tр╢║5р╢╕ р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╢з р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒ р╖Гр╖Пр╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢лMр╖Ар╢║ р╢Й^ "#р╢╕, ┬╡├в р╢╢р╖Щр╖А' р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щр╖Ер╢▒ Tр╢║5 р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╖Щ$ ┬╡├в р╢╢р╖А р╢Ер╖Ар╖Г' "#р╢╕, р╢Т р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ р╖Гр╖КS Lр╖В р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢вр╢╖р╖Пр╖Ар╢║ р╖Ер╢Яр╖П р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖Пр╖А' р╖Гр╖Д р╖Еg' р╖Гр╢╢р╢╜ р╢Ьр╖Р'Jр╢╕ р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╖Щ. р╢┤р╢▒M р╖Щр╢Ъ^.р╢┤р╢н р╢╕├Ч' р╢Й^ "#р╢╕р╢з р╢Ер╢┤ р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╢╗1M р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖П р╢Ър╢╗ р╢ЬN7', Tр╢║5 р╖Щ р╖Б~*р╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Гр╢▒р╢║' р╢ЙXр╢║р╢з р╢З? р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╢║р╢з -р╢┤┬бQр╢║ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╖Щ0 р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╢║ р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Щ р╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Гр╢▒ р╢З? ┬Яр╢лр╖П.- р╢Ър╢з "#р╢╕M р╖Щр╢╕р╢╕ ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╖Щ р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤M J ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╗gp 17 р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' g р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║р╢╕ р╢С р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Др╢▒р╢Ър╢з р╖Щр╢║1g р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ р╖Щ. р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖ЩH0 р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖Пр╖А', р╢нLр╢лU' р╖Др╖П р╢пLр╖А' р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' р╖Щр╖Бnр╖В р╢Ер╖Ар╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢║1g "#р╢╕ р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ер╢п р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║р╢зр╢╕ ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Б J ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щр╢╕ р╢╗р╖Пр╢в р╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢Ър╢║' р╢Т р╢╢р╖А Eр╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╖Ср╢╕ р╢╗р╢зр╢Ър╢зр╢╕ р╢Ер╖Ар╖БU. р╢▒gM ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢▒1р╢╕р╖Р?р╖А T┬╡ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╖Ар╖Пр╢┤р╖Ш? р╢╕├Ч' NT %р╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢Ь'р╢▒р╢з р╢Ер╢╕р╖ПLU. р╢Ер╢п р╖Щ. р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖ЩH р╢Ер╢пр╖Др╖Гр╖К р╢пр╖Рu р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖АL, Nр╖Щр╢║р╢в р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖АL, р╢╕'Sр╖АL р╖Др╖Рр╢╕ р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╢╕ р╢ЪLp р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Щр╖Еn, р╢░р╖Пр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Щр╢║' р╖Гр╢│р╖Д' р╢Ър╖Щр╖Еn, р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╢вр╖П?р╢Ъ р╖Г.р╢┤M Iр╢Ър╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒, р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ -р╖Гр╢нр╖П T┬Яр╢┤р╖Пр╖Ар╖П,

р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А

р╢Ьр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Е- Iр╢Ър╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Ер╢Ър╢з р╖Щр╢║1g р╢║ U "р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ср╢ЪU. р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢ЬL р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Р? р╢╕р╖П р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ Iр╢Ъ р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╢Ър╢╗р╖П р╢║'р╢▒U р╖Гр╖Ср╢╕ р╢зр╢╕ р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ'.

р╢ЙX р╖А&р╖В 15р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╖Е Tр╢║5р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╢з р╖Щр╢┤1┬╡р╖ЩH р╖Гр╢╕р╖Ш р╖Щр╢║', р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖РMр╢╕ р╢║р╖Др╢┤Mр╖А р╢нр╢╢р╖П р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║р╢╕ р╢С J р╢З? р╢Ър╢╗ р╢ЬM р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖А р╢ЕVр╖А ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╖Г р╢╗р╖П р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕ р╢Ер╢┤ Tр╢║5 р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╢зр╢╕ р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. E├Ър╢Ър╢╕ р╢╗' "#р╢╕, sр╖Г Q'р╢▒ ^ р╢пр╖Рvр╢╕, р╢║р╖Др╢┤M р╖Щр╖Г┬Юр╢Ыр╢║ р╖Др╖П Nр╖Щр╢╗├в р╢┤р╖Рр╖Ар╖РMр╢╕, ~р╢лр╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ер╢░р╖Пр╢┤р╢▒р╢║, р╖Гр╖КS Lр╖В р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢вр╢╖р╖Пр╖Ар╢║ р╢Ж0 р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║' р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ 17 ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ър╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢З р╖ЕM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ср╢╕ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╢вр╢║ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕ р╢Ер╢┤ Tр╢║5 р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ р╢ЕR%р╖Пр╢║ р╢║ U. р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒M р╢╗р╢зр╖Ар╢╜ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ р╢░ р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Щ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Б E' ┬йр╢з р╖Щр╢┤р╢╗M р╢░ р╖Ар╖Рр╢йр╖Гр╢зр╖Д' ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖ЕM, р╢╕р╢╕ 2р╢нр╢▒ р╢║р╢з р╖Щ. р╖Ар╢▒ LM "Tр╢╕ р╢╗р╢зр╢Ър╢з р╢нр╖Ар╢╕M ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Г├Ър╢╕ р╢╜р╖Р┬╗ р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╢нр╢╕U р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ р╖Гр╢Вр╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╢╕├Ч' р╖Щ. р╢Жр╢Ър╖Пр╢╗р╖Щ р╢║р╖Ар╢╗ р╢Ь'р╢▒р╢з Tр╢║5р╢╕ р╢╗р╢зр╖А! р╢Ер╢п р╢Ср╢Ър╢Яр╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢Ър╢з р╢З!р╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢'р╖Щ'.

?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╖Ер╢Яр╖П р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╖Щ.0 р╖ГMMр╖АU' р╖Др╖П р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ р╖Гр╢╕р╢Я ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░р╢║ р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ьр╢╗ р╖Г.р╢┤M ┬бр╢╗mр╢нр╢нр╖Пр╖А 14 р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║' р╖Д├Ъ'р╖Ар╖П 0 ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Ар╢▒ ┬╣J' р╢З р╖Ар╢▒ р╖Г.р╢┤M Iр╢Ъ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕ 15 р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╖Ар╖Бр╖Щр╢║' р╖Д├Ъ'р╖Ар╖П 0 ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╖Щ0 р╖Гр╢нр╖П T┬Яр╢┤р╖Пр╖А'р╢з, р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╢пр╖Ар╢▒ р╢Ер╖Ар╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ер╢┤р╖Щ$ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║ р╢ЙX р╖Ар╖Гр╢╗ 15 р╖Е t р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖Пр╖А р╖Е ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╢вр╢║ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╖Щ. ┬бр╖Г! р╢ЕRр╖Щр╢║р╢Ьр╢║ р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢ЬL р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕р╖П р╖Ар╖П  р╖Щр╢▒1р╢╢р╢╜р╖П, р╢Ер╖Щ= Nр╢╜р╢░р╖ПX' р╖Гр╢╕р╢Я Nр╢╗'р╢нр╢╗р╖Щр╢║' р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢╗р╢зр╖А! 133р╢Ъ %р╢░р╖ПN' 2015 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& р╢╕р╖Пр╖Гр╖Щ0 NHр╖Щр╢║& Vр╖Ар╢╗ р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ ┬вр╢╜р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╢║р╢з р╢С J ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ 17 р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║р╢з р╢СE р╢пр╖Рuр╖Ар╖П. р╢Ер╢┤р╖Щ$ р╢Е?р╢ЬL р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢┤? р╢╕р╖Пр╢п р╢Ср╢╕ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╖Гр╖Др╢╖р╖ПQ Jр╢╕ р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM T┬╡Jр╢╕. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢┤Xр╢лр╖Пр╢╕р╖Щ0 р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖Пр╖А' р╖Др╖П р╢Ьр╖Рр╖Др╖РV р╖Еg' р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╢Е'р╢н&р╢Ьр╢н р╢║ U. р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ър╢Ьр╢н р╢╕р╢▒р╖П р╖Щр╖Гnр╖Ар╖Пр╖А' р╢Фр╖Гр╖Кр╖Щр╖Гn р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖Пр╖А'р╖Щ$ р╖Др╖П р╢Ф┬Я'р╖Щ$ р╢┤┬Я!р╖Ар╢╜ р╖Щр╖Г┬Юр╢Ыр╢║ р╖Гр╖Д р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖Пр╖А р╖Ар╖Р├Б  p "#р╢╕р╢з р╖Др╖Р" р╖Ар╢▒ р╢Ер╢нр╢╗, р╢╡р╢╜р╢пр╖П├г р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Ар╢▒ р╖Др╖П р╖Ыр╢пNр╢Ъ р╢Ър╖П&р╢║р╢║' р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╖Ар╖Рр╢║ р╢Ър╢╗V р╖Щр╖АVр╖Ар╢з р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢в, р╢Ж&iр╢Ъ р╖Др╖П р╖Щ р╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╢Ър╢з р╖Ар╢╜ Nр╢╗р╢н Jр╢╕р╢з Nр╢пр╖Др╖Г р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╕р╢з ├Вр╢╗р╢лр╢║ "#р╢╕ р╖Е р╖Гр╖Др╢╖р╖ПQMр╖Ар╢║ р╢З р╢нр╖АM %?р╢╜р╖Пр╢╖ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢Ьр╢н р╖Др╖Р"U.

р╢┤р╖Ер╖ПM р╖Гр╢╖р╖П р╢╕р╖Р?р╖Ар╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░р╖Щр╢║' р╢Кр╖Щ р╢пр╖Ар╖Щр╖Гn р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╢вр╢║ р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╖Е р╢┤р╢▒M р╖Щр╢Ъ^.р╢┤р╢н -р╢Ър╢╜ ?р╖Гр╖Кр╖Щр╖Гn р╢ЙXр╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗ р╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╖А- р╖Г.р╢╕р╢н р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ь'р╢▒ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╖А'р╢Ър╢╕ р╢╜р╖Рzр╢лр╖П. р╖Щ р╖Бр╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╖Щр╖Вn├Яр╢║ р╖Е, р╢┤р╖Ер╖ПM р╖Гр╢╖р╖П, р╢┤р╖Ер╖ПM р╢┤р╖Пр╢╜р╢▒ р╢Жр╢║р╢нр╢▒ р╖Др╖П р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А р╖Е Tр╢║р╢║р╢з 25р╢Ъ р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖П Nр╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒р╢║ р╢╜р╢╢р╖П 0р╢╕ Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Е р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╖Г ^ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Ь. р╢╕р╢╕ р╢┤┬бQр╢║ р╖Ар╖Гр╖Щ& р╢Е?р╢ЬL р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╢┤? р╢╕р╖П р╖Гр╢╕р╢Я р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ р╖Гр╢Вр╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╖Щ р╢╕р╖Др╖П р╢╕`р╢йр╢╜ р╖Гр╖РTр╖Ар╖Пр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░ ┬Яр╢л р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖Пр╖ЩH р╢╕р╢з р╢╕р╢нр╢ЪU, р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢╗р╢зр╖Ар╢╜ р╢Ер╖Ар╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║р╢з р╖Щр╢║1g р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?zр╢л %р╢░р╖Пр╢▒ р╖Щ р╢нр╢╕U ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║. р╖Щр╢╕1р╢Ър╢п, р╢Ер╢п р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╖Щр╢╕1р╢▒ р╢нр╢╗. р╢Ър╖П&┬йр╢Ър╢╗р╢лр╢║ ┬Яр╢лM, р╢Ър╖Шm р╢Ър╖П&7р╢Ъ р╢Е&iр╢Ъ р╢╗р╢зр╖Пр╖А р╢┤р╖Рр╖А р╢лM, р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒M р╖Щр╖Гnр╖Ар╖П E' р╢╗р╢зр╖А! р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ ┬Яр╢лM ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢▒1р╢╕р╖Р?р╢Ър╢╕ Nр╖Гр╖П р╢Ер╢п р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╢ЕRр╖Щр╢║р╢Ьр╖Ар╢╜р╢з g┬Шр╢л 0р╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т р╢ЕRр╖Щр╢║р╢Ь р╢вр╢║р╢Ь'р╢▒ р╢Зр╢нр╖Р. р╢╗р╢зр╖А! р╢ЛMр╖Гр╖Пр╖Д р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Лр╢пр╖Пр╖Др╢╗р╢лр╢║р╢Ър╢з р╢Е ├╜р╢▒р╢║ р╢ЬNg. ├╜р╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╖Ар╖Р├Бр╢╕ р╢вр╢▒р╢Ьр╖Др╢▒р╢║ р╢Й'р╢▒ р╢╗р╢з ┬Яр╢лM, р╢Ер╖Др╖Г р╢Лр╖Гр╢з р╖А р╢║р╢▒ р╖Бр╖Пр╢╜ р╖Щр╢Ь1р╢йр╢▒р╖Р├ЧD р╢Й р╢Ър╖ЕM, р╢Е р╢п'р╢▒р╖Ар╖П р╢Т р╢╗р╖Щx р╢Т р╢Т р╖Щр╢Ъ1xр╢ир╖Пр╖Гр╖Ар╢╜ р╖Щр╖А' р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Лр╢пр╖Пр╢▒, р╖Ар╢▒ р╖Ар╢Ьр╖П, р╢Т р╢Ср╢Ър╢╕ р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║р╢з 2р╢нр╢Ър╢╗ р╖Щ р╖А! ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╢╗7' T┬Вр╢▒ р╢╢р╖А.

┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒M р╢╗р╖Пр╢вр╢║' E' ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Е р╢С'р╢▒р╢з р╢ЪD' р╖Щ. р╢╗р╢вр╢║ р╢Т р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╢╕ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║ р╢┤M р╢Ър╖Е р╢╢р╖А р╢╕р╖П р╖Щр╖Бnр╖Вр╖Щр╢║'р╢╕ р╖Гр╢│р╖Д' р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╢Хр╢▒р╖С.

р╢Ср╖Щр╖Гn р╢┤M р╢Ър╢╗р╢╜р╖П р╖Щ. р╢╗р╖Щx р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Б 52р╢Ъ р╖Др╖П р╢╗р╖Пр╢в р╢Жр╢║р╢нр╢▒ р╖Др╖Пр╢╗Tр╢║ р╢Ьр╢лр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢Ср╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╖Р┬В ┬Яp, р╢╢ р╢░ ┬Яp, р╢Т E' р╖Щр╢┤р╖Вр╢лр╢║ ┬Яp р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╖Гр╖П&р╢ор╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Е р╢Ър╢╗р╖П р╢Ьр╢╕' р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢Тр╖Щр╢Ъ0 р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╢╗р╢зр╖Ар╢╜р╢з, р╢╗р╖Пр╢в р╢▒р╖Пр╢║р╢ЪU'р╢з р╖Ар╢йр╖П р╢Е р╢ЙXр╖Щр╢║' T┬В7' р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ ┬др╢║р╖П р╢╕р╖П&р╢Ьр╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢ЕVр╢Ьр╢н р╖Щр╖А7' р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╖Ер╖П.

р╢Ер╢п р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢╗р╢зр╖Ар╢╜ р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╢з ┬Шр╖Гр╖Кр╢╕ р╢Ь'р╢▒ XT┬╡ р╖Ар╖Пр╢нр╢║ р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢Ер╢п g┬Шр╢п р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╢▒р╢╗р╢Ъ р╢║р╢з р╢Е XT┬╡ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П; g┬Ш┬╡ р╖Щр╖Ар╢╗р╖Е р╢Ер╢┤├Я р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П; р╢вр╢╜р╢║ р╢Ер╢┤├Я р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Гр╢╕р╖Др╢╗ %р╖Щ р╖Бр╖Ар╢╜ 7Nр╖Гр╖К┬б р╖Щр╢╢1'р╢▒ р╖А р╢╗ ┬Вр╢Ъ р╢▒р╖Р?р╖А р╖Гр╖Рр╢н . р╢Ьр╢л' ┬╡р╢╗ р╢║р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢Ьр╢║ р╖Щр╢п1р╢╗ р╖Др╢пр╢▒р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╢з р╢Е р╢Тр╖Ар╖П Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╖Гр╖Рр╢╜"!р╢╜ р╢пр╖А'р╖Щ' р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢Ср╖Щр╢▒р╢пр╖П ┬╣р╖АM Jр╢╕ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢┤р╢╕р╢л Tр╢нр╖П р╢Ър╖Рр╢╜р╖С -р╖Ар╢▒р╖П'р╢нр╢╗- р╢▒р╖Пр╖Б "#р╢╕ р╖Е р╢З? ┬Яp р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д T┬╡J. ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢┤┬б Qр╢║ р╢╗р╢вр╢║ р╢Лр╢╕р╖П р╢Фр╢║ р╖Ар╖Пр╢┤р╖Ш?р╢║ р╢Жр╢╗.р╢╖ "#р╖Щ.0 р╖ДXр╢║р╢з р╖Бр╢Ър╢нр╖П р╢Ер╢░р╢║р╢▒ р╖Ар╖П&р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖АM -feasibility report- р╢▒р╖Р?р╖АU р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢'р╖Щ' "р╢║р╢▒ р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Ер╢п р╢┤р╖Рр╖Др╖РDр╖А р╢пр╖Рр╢▒ р╢Ь'р╢▒ р╢╜р╖Р┬╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

р╖Щ. р╢╗ р╖Щx р╢Ер╖Др╖Гр╢з р╢Лр╖Гр╢з р╖Щр╢Ь1р╢йр╢▒р╖Р├ЧD р╖Др╖Р┬╡р╢лM, р╖Щр╢╕1р╢▒ р╢нр╢╗. р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ ┬др╢║р╖Пр╢пр╖Пр╢╕р╢║' T┬╡ ┬Яр╢лM р╖Щ. р╢╗р╢зр╢з р╢Жр╖ЩH*р╢Ъ р╖Гр╢Вр╖Гр╖Кр╢Ър╖Ш?р╢║ р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢╢р╖Р├Ъp, р╢╢ р╢░ ┬Яp р╢Й?р╖Др╖Пр╖Гр╢║ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢пр╢пр╖Др╖Гр╖К р╢┤'Tр╢║ р╖Ар╖Гр╢╗р╢Ъ р╢Ир╢н р╢Й?р╖Др╖Пр╖Гр╢║р╢Ъ р╢ЕRр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒, р╖Щр╢╢┬Ю р╢░ fр╖Вр╖Кр╢зр╖Пр╢ар╖Пр╢╗р╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒, Tр╢Вр╖Др╢╜ р╖Гр╢Вр╖Гр╖Кр╢Ър╖Ш?р╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╖Щр╢пр╢▒s р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢ЕVр╢╗р╖Пр╢░ р╢╗, р╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╖Е1'р╢▒L р╢Ь р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒

р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢пр╢╣р╖Щр╢пN р╢Ьр╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢Т р╢Ср╢Ър╢╕ р╢З? ┬Яp N&р╢╕р╖Пр╢лр╢║' Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢Ср╢пр╖П ?zр╢лр╖П р╖Ар╖Рр╖АU р╢пр╖П р╢Ьр╖Рр╢╢U р╢Ьр╢╕U р╢┤'р╖Гр╢╜U "р╢║р╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╖Гр╖Кр╢Ър╖Ш?р╢║. р╖Щр╢╕р╢нр╖Рр╢▒0 р╢┤'р╖Гр╢╜ "р╢║р╢╜р╖П р╢ЬMр╢нр╖Пр╢з р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒M р╢Жр╢Ь7р╢Ъ р╢╕р╢░р╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╢▒р╢║ ┬Яр╢лM ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖А'. р╢Т р╖Гр╢Вр╖Гр╖Кр╢Ър╖Ш?р╢║ Nр╖Гр╖П g р╢Ьр╢╕ р╖Др╖Р┬╡р╢лр╖П. р╢Ьр╢╕ р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╢▒р╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Рр╖А ?zр╢лр╖П, р╢нр╖А р╢нр╖Рр╢▒р╢Ъ р╢пр╖П р╢Ьр╖Рр╢╢ ?zр╢лр╖П. 7N┬б'р╖Щ$ TM р╖Гр╢н'р╖Ар╢╜р╢з р╢╕р╖Пр╢▒Tр╢Ъ р╖Гр╖Др╢▒р╢║, 'р╢пр╢▒р╢║ р╢Т E' р╢╜р╢╢р╖П р╢Ь'р╢▒р╢з р╢Ер╖Ар╖Гр╖Кр╢ор╖Пр╖А N&р╢╕р╖Пр╢лр╢║ р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?zр╢лр╖П. р╢Ср╢нр╖РN' р╢Ср╖Др╖Пр╢з р╢ЬMр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╢Ьр╢╕ р╖Щр╢Ър╖Ер╖Ар╖Щ& р╢Ър╖Рр╢╜р╖Ср╖А ?zр╢лр╖П; р╖Ар╖ПX р╢Ъ&р╢╕р╖П'р╢н ?zр╢лр╖П. 7N┬б' р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║р╢з р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕ р╢Жр╢пр╢╗р╢║ р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢Ьр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Е р╢Ър╢┤р╢▒ р╖Щр╢Ър╖Щр╢▒s р╖Гр╢╕р╖Др╢╗ р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖Пр╖Ар╢з р╢╗┬В' ^р╖Ар╖Д! р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╢нр╢╗р╢╕р╢з р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╢нр╢пр╢╢р╢╜ \? ?zр╢лр╖П. р╢▒gM, р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║ ?р╖Гр╖Кр╖Щр╖Гn р╖Щ. р╢╗р╖Щx р╖Щр╢╕1р╢Ър╢п ┬Яр╖Щ`? р╢╕р╢░р╢╕ р╢Ъ├Ър╢Ър╢╗р╢║ р╢ЬMр╢нM, р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒M %р╖Щ р╖Б р╢ЬMр╢нM р╢Ер╢п р╢Т Tр╢║!р╢╜ р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Е27 р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╢║ р╖Ар╖Пр╢┤р╖Ш? Nр╖Гр╖П р╢нр╢╗ р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╖АU, р╢Т р╖Др╖П р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░ р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╢Ър╢з Nр╖Гр╖П р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Е27 ┬Яp р╖Щр╢╢1р╖Щр╖Д р╖Щ р╖А! р╢▒р╖Рр╖Ар╢н р╖Др╢п'р╢▒ р╖А'р╢Ър╢╕ р╢▒р╖Р? р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╢║ р╖Щ. р╖Др╖П р╢╢р╢╜'р╢▒р╢з р╢ЪD' р╖Щр╢╕├Фр╢ар╢╗ р╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ъ р╖Г.р╢┤Mр╖АD' р╢Е├пр╢л, р╢Ьр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Ер╢з, р╖Гр╢нр╖П┬╖р╢┤р╖Пр╖Ар╖Пр╢з, р╢Зр╖Е р╖Щр╢п1р╖Ер╢з -р╢Т Tр╢║!р╢╜р╢з- р╢Жр╢пр╢╗р╢║ р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ 7N┬б' t р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖Пр╖ЩH N&р╢╕р╖Пр╢лр╢║ "#р╢╕ %р╢░р╖Пр╢▒ р╢Ъ&р╢нр╖Ар╢║ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤M р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

р╖Щ. р╢Ър╖П&р╢║р╖Щ0 р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Йр╢нр╖П р╖Щр╢╜1s р╖Ар╢Ьvр╢╕ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Щ. р╢Ър╖П&р╢║р╖Щ0 р╢Т Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢Лр╢┤р╖Щр╢пр╖Гр╖К р╖Щр╢п'р╢▒ р╖А' р╢║. (Dr.) Nalinda Jayathissa) ┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╖Ар╖Рр╢пр╢ЬM, ! р╖Гр╖Д р╖Гр╢В р╢н р╖Вр╢║р╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│р╖АU р╢Ер╢п р╢Ер╢┤ р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ъ├Фр╢бр╖П р╢Ър╢╗7' р╢Й'р╖Щ'. ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ "р╢║р╢▒ р╖Вр╢║ р╢┤р╢ор╢║р╢з р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖А' р╖Щр╢╜1sр╢╕ р╢Ер╖Гр╖Пр╢░р╖Пр╢╗р╢лр╢║ р╢нр╢╕U, р╢Ср╢║ р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗ р╖Щр╖Д р╖Ар╢▒┬╣J р╖Щр╖Д р╖Ар╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╢╗р╖Вр╢л р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║M р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢╢ р╢░ р╢Ър╢╗ ?┬╗р╢╕. р╢Тр╢Ъ р╢Зр╢╕?р╖Ар╢╗р╢║р╖Пр╢з р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Щ$ р╖Щр╢ар╢пр╢▒р╖Пр╖А р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╖АU. р╢▒gM ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ "р╢║р╢▒ р╖Вр╢║ р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗ р╖Щр╖Д р╖Ар╢▒ р╖Гр╢Вр╢╗р╖Вр╢лр╢║M р╢Ср╢Ъ р╢╢ р╢░ р╢Ър╖Ер╖Пр╢з р╢┤┬бр╖А р╢ЬL р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢н р╢╕N, р╢Т р╖Вр╢║ р╢┤^ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╖Щ.р╢Ъ Nр╢Ъ. р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║M р╢Ср╢Ъ, р╢Ьр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖ЕM р╢Ср╢Ъ, р╖Гр╢нр╖П T┬Яр╢┤р╖Пр╖Ар╖ПM р╢Ср╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$ р╖Г.р╢╢'р╢░ р╖Вр╢║р╢║ 7р╖Г, р╢Ср╢нр╖РN' р╢Ср╖Др╖Пр╢з Qр╢║ ! р╖Вр╢║р╢║ р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤M р╖Щр╖А'р╢▒ 2р╢н'р╢▒ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ р╢Йр╢йр╢Ър╢й р╢нр╢╕U р╢Е27

р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢'р╖Щ'. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ "р╢║'р╖Щ', р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Хр╢▒р╖Ср╢╕ р╢Ер╢║ р╖Ар╖Рр╢║р╢Ър╢з р╢┤р╢пр╢▒. р╖Щр╖А'р╢▒ р╢Хр╢▒р╖С, р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Хр╢▒р╖Ср╢╕ ┬вDр╢Ъ \?р╢║р╢Ър╢з р╢┤р╢пр╢▒. р╖Щр╖А'р╢▒ р╢Хр╢▒р╖С, р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢Хр╢▒р╖Ср╢╕ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╢║р╢Ъ р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Ер╢Ър╢з р╢┤р╢пр╢▒. р╖Щр╖А'р╢▒ р╢Хр╢▒р╖С !, р╢Йр╢нр╖Пр╢╕ р╢пр╖Рр╖Ар╖Р'р╢н р╖Ар╖Рр╢й Eр╖Щр╖Ар╖Е; р╖Вр╢║ р╢┤р╢ор╢║. р╢Т Nр╖Гр╖П р╢нр╢╕U р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П├В'р╖Щ$ р╖Гр╢Вр╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╖Д р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢╗р╖Пр╢в р╢╕р╖Рр╖ДM р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П, ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ер╢╗gр╢л 17 р╖Гр╖Д р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ 169 р╢┤р╢пр╢▒. р╢Ър╢╗р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╖Щ. Dр╢║!р╢╜ р╖Гр╢Ър╖Гр╖К р╢Ър╢╗ ?р╖Щр╢╢'р╖Щ'. р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖Щ$ р╢вр╢▒ ┬╣р╢нр╢║ р╢▒р╢Яр╖П T^р╖А'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п; ┬╡=р╢┤Mр╢Ър╢╕ р╢╗' р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п; р╢Ер╢░р╖Пр╢┤р╢▒р╢║, р╖Щр╖Г┬Юр╢Ыр╢║ р╢▒р╢Яр╖П T^р╖А'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п; р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п; р╢Ер╖Щ= р╖Щр╢Ь1р╢й┬Чр╢╕ р╖Гр╖Д р╢вр╢╜ р╖Г.р╢┤р╢н р╢Жр╢╗р╖Вр╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Щр╖Д1р╢╕р╢п "р╢║р╢▒ р╖Щ. р╢ЪLp Tр╢║!р╢╜ -р╢╕р╖Пр╢▒р╖Ар╢║р╖Пр╢з р╖Щ. 72р╢нр╢╜р╢║ р╢╕р╢н р╖Ар╖Пр╖Гр╢║ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒, р╖Щр╢пр╢┤U' р╢▒р╖Р┬е T┬В'р╢▒, р╢Ф┬Шр╖Щ$ ┬╣р╢нр╢║ р╢┤р╖АMр╖Ар╖П р╖Щр╢Ьр╢▒ р╢║'р╢▒р╢з р╢Ер╖Ар╖Б р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ Tр╢║5 р╖Щ р╖А!- р╢Ер╢йр╢В~ р╢┤р╖Рр╖Щр╢вр╢║ р╢нр╢╕U ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ р╢║р╢зр╖ЩM р╖Д├Ъ'р╖Ар╖П 0 ?р╖Щ'р╖Щ'.

┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╢пр╖Р' р╖Щ. р╢╕р╖П р╢Ер╖ЩM ?р╖Щр╢╢'р╖Щ' р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╢Ъ.р╢ЪL р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нр╖Пр╢Вр╖Бр╖ЩM р╢╕р╖Рр╖ДMJр╢╕ р╢╕р╢н р╖Гр╢Ър╖Гр╖К р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒ р╢╜р╢п р╖Ар╖П&р╢нр╖Пр╖А. р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╢Ер╢░р╖Пр╢┤р╢▒р╢║р╢з р╢З р╖ЕM р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Ар╢▒ р╢пLр╖А' Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Т р╖Ар╖П&р╢нр╖Пр╖ЩH р╖Гр╢│р╖Д' р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╖Гр╖Пр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒р╖Щр╢║' р╢Е┬ЯL р╢пр╢Ър╢з р╢┤р╖Пр╖Г! р╢║р╖П р╖Ар╢║р╖Щр╖Гn р╢пLр╖А'р╖Щр╢Ь' Tр╢║р╢║р╢з 90.1 р╢┤р╖Пр╖Г! р╢Ер╢░р╖Пр╢┤р╢▒р╢║р╢з р╢З р╖ЕM р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╢з р╢нр╖АM Tр╢║р╢║р╢з 9.9 р╢┤р╖Пр╖Г! р╢Ер╢░р╖Пр╢┤р╢▒р╖Щр╢║' р╢╢р╖Рр╖Др╖Рр╢╗ р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

р╢Жр╢пр╖Пр╢║р╢╕ р╖Ар╖Р├Б р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕р╢з р╢┤р╢╕р╢л р╖Щр╢▒1р╖Щр╖АU; р╢╗р╖Щx р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╖Щр╖Г┬Юр╢Ы р╖Г.р╢┤'р╢▒ "#р╢╕р╢з р╖Гр╖Д р╢╗р╖Щx р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖Щ$ р╢┤├Б р╢┤р╖Щр╢н' р╢Жр╖Др╖Пр╢╗ р╢┤р╖Пр╢▒ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢║р╢▒ р╢║р╢пр╢╕ р╢Еa р╢Ър╢╗ р╢Ьр╖Р\р╖Щ. р╢Ер╢╗gр╢л р╖Г2р╢нр╖АU.

р╢Е р╢╢р╖Р5р╖Щр╖А1M р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ', р╖Щр╢╜р╢Ър╖Щ р╢Хр╢▒р╖Ср╢╕ р╢╗р╢зр╢Ъ р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖А р╖Щ$ ┬вDр╢Ъ р╢Жр╖Др╖Пр╢╗ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢║р╢▒ р╢║р╢п. р╢Еa р╢╢р╖А. р╖Др╖Рр╢╢р╖РU, р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╖Щx р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖Щ$ р╖Ар╖Р^р╖Щр╢┤' Tр╢║р╢║р╢з 60р╢Ър╢з р╢Жр╖Г'р╢▒ %р╢╕р╖Пр╢лр╢║ р╢║р╢п. р╖Щр╖А'р╖Щ' р╢Ъ'р╢▒ р╖Щр╢╢1'р╢▒ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Б р╖Щ р╖А! р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖ПU. р╢Ср╢╕ Nр╖Гр╖П р╢Ър╖Шm р╢Ъ&р╢╕р╖П'р╢нр╢║ Eр╢╢р╢│р╖А р╢Ер╖Ар╢░р╖Пр╢▒р╢║ р╖Щр╢║1g р╢Ър╢╗'р╖Щ' р╢▒р╖Р?р╖А ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Йр╢╜р╢Ъ Eр╢╢р╢│ р╖Гр╖Пр╢Ъ├Фр╢бр╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╢╢р╖Рр╖Др╖Р.

р╢Е р╢Е┬ЯL┬╡ р╢Ьр╢лр╢▒р╖Пр╖А ?р╖Гр╖Кр╖Щр╖Гn р╖Гр╖Пр╢╕р╖Пр╢▒р╖Щр╢║' р╢Е┬ЯL р╢пр╢Ър╢з 260,000 275,000 р╢┤р╢╕р╢л р╖Щр╢пр╢▒р╖П р╖Щ р╖Б I"р╢║р╖П р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П р╢║р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢СU' р╖Ар╖Р├Б р╖Гр╢Вр╢Ыр╖Пр╖А р╢Ър╖П'р╢нр╖Пр╖А'. р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╢Ь'р╢▒ р╖Щр╢Ъ1р╖Ер╢╣ р╢Ъ^р╖Щр╢Ьр╢║ р╢Е5Mр╖Ар╖Р├Бр╢║р╖П р╢Ър╖Ер╖П. р╢Т р╢Ъ^р╖Щр╢ЬU ?zp р╢┤р╖Рр╢╗* р╢╗р╖Пр╢вvр╢║ р╢Ъaр╖Ар╢з р╢Ер╢п р╖Ар╢▒ р╢зM р╖Щр╖А├Фр╢а р╖Щр╢пр╢║ р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. ┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╢Ср╖Щр╖Др╢╕ р╢нр╢╕U р╢╗р╖Пр╢вр╢┤р╖Вр╖АL р╢Ер╢▒р╖Пр╢Ьр╢н р╢┤р╢╗ р╢╗ р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' р╢Т р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╖Щ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒ р╢Ър╢з р╢Ър╖Щр╖Еn.

р╢Т р╢╗р╖Пр╢вр╢┤р╖В р╢Ьр╢║ р╖Др╖Р┬╜'uр╖Щ "р╢Жр╖Бр╖Кр╢а&р╢║р╖Щ р╢Ьр╢║" "р╢║р╢╜р╖ПU. р╢Ср╖Щр╖Гn р╢Жр╖Бр╖Кр╢а&р╢║р╖Щ р╢Ьр╢║р╢з Qр╢║р╖П р╢▒. р╢Ер╢┤р╢з р╢нр╢╢р╖П р╢Ср╖ГM р╢вр╖П?'р╢з р╖АM р╖Щ. t р╢╜р╢Вр╢Ър╖Пр╖А р╖Е ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╢Ьр╖Рр╢▒ р╢Ър╢нр╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖Щр╖Д р╢Т р╖Щр╖АVр╖Щр╖А' ┬др╢║р╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖Щр╖Д р╖Щр╢пр╢║ р╢Й?X р╖А'р╖Щ' р╢▒р╖Рр╖Др╖Р. р╢┤┬б Qр╢║ р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╢║ р╢Ер╖Ар╖Г' ┬Яр╖Щ` р╢Ер╖Щ= р╢╗р╢з р╢Зр╖Щр╢╕Xр╢Ър╖ПV р╖Щр╢й1р╢╜& ┬ЧDр╢║р╢▒ 10,000р╢Ъ р╢лр╢║р╢ЪLр╖Аs р╢╢р╖Ар╢з р╢┤M р╖Щр╖А7'. р╢С2 р╢┤р╖А р╢нр╢╕U р╢Ер╢пр╢зM р╢Е р╖Щ. р╖Щр╢Ьр╖А'р╖Щ'. р╢Т р╢Ьр╖Щ р╢Жр╖Бр╖Кр╢а&р╢║р╢║ р╖Ер╢В р╖Щр╖Ар╢╜р╖П ?zр╢лр╖П р╢▒., р╢Т р╢╗р╖Пр╢вр╢┤р╖В р╢┤┬Я!р╖Ар╢╜ р╢Ер╢║р╢з, 2р╢н 7 р╢╗'р╢з р╖Гр╖Д р╖Щр╢Ьр╢╜ р╢╢р╖Пр╢╜р╢║'р╢з р╢нр╢╗U. р╢Т р╢║р╢з р╢нр╢╕U р╢Т р╢Ър╖Пр╢╜р╖Щ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ ┬др╢║р╖ПMр╢╕р╢Ъ ┬Яр╖Щ`.

┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╢Е р╖Щ. р╢┤р╢▒р╢н р╢╕├Ч' р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╢╗1M р╖Щр╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П, ?р╢╗р╖Гр╢╗ р╖Гр╢Вр╖А&р╢░р╢▒р╢║ р╖Гр╢│р╖Др╖П Nр╖Ар╖РI %?р╢┤M? р╖Др╖П р╢Лр╢┤р╖Пр╢║ р╢╕р╖П&р╢Ь р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ \?р╢╕р╢║ р╢╗р╖Пgр╖А р╖Гр╢Ър╖Гр╖К р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒; р╢Т р╖Ар╖Пр╖Щ$р╢╕ р╖Гр╖Кр╖Ар╖Пр╢╖р╖Пр╢Ъ, р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢в├гр╢║ р╖Др╖П р╢Ж&iр╢Ъ р╖Г.р╢┤M р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗ 2р╢нр╢Ър╖П7 р╖Щр╢╜р╖Г р╢Ър╖П&р╢║р╖Вр╢╕р╖А р╢┤Xр╖Др╢╗р╢лр╢║ "#р╢╕ р╖Гр╖Д?р╢Ъ р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒; р╢Ж`aр╖ЩH Tр╢║5 ├Вр╢╗р╢л р╢Ьр╖Р\.р╖Ар╢╜0 р╢┤Xр╖Гр╢╗р╢║ р╖Др╖П р╢Ер╖Щр╢▒sM р╖Гр╢╕р╖Пр╢в├гр╢║ р╢ЪLp р╢Тр╢Ър╖Пр╢╢ р╢░ р╖Ар╢▒ р╢┤X ├Вр╢╗р╢л р╢Ь'р╢▒. р╢Т р╢Ер╖Ар╖Бр╢нр╖П р╖Г р╢╗р╖Пр╢Ьр╖Р\р╢╕р╢з р╖Щ. р╢┤р╢▒р╢н р╢╕├Ч' р╢Е р╢╢р╢╜р╖Пр╖Щр╢┤1р╖Щр╢╗1M р╖Ар╢▒р╖Ар╖П.

Presiding Member) ┬вр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П├Юр╢к р╢ЬL р╢╕'S р╢╕N, р╖Гр╢╖р╖Пр╖А р╢Ъ! р╢нр╖Р┬╗р╖Щ. р╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╖А р╢ЙXр╢┤M "#р╢╕ р╢ЬL р╢С..р╢С├Ф.р╢С.. р╖Г!р╢╕р╖П' р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П. р╖Щр╢╗G?р╢Ьeр╖П р╢вр╢▒р╢нр╖Пр╖Ар╖Щ┬В р╢Ьр╖Рр╢зz Iр╖Г┬пр╢╕р╢з Oр╢║р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗ р╢╗р╢вр╢║р╢з р╢╢р╢╜ }`р╢╕ рпЗро░ро╛ро╣ро┐'роХро┐ропро╛ роороХро│ро┐ рокро┐ро░ роЪро┐рпИрой родрпА54 рооро┐ропрооро╛5 роЕро░рпИроЪ ро╡89.род2 URGE GOVERNMENT OF MYANMAR TO FIND SOLUTIONS TO PROBLEMS OF ROHINGYA PEOPLE р╢Ь. р╢С. р╢С┬З. р╢С. р╖Г;р╢╕р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ роО.роО/.роО. роЪ8рооро╛) (The Hon. M.H.M. Salman) Hon. Presiding Member, I move, тАЬWhereas the escalating conflict in certain parts of Myanmar has resulted in loss of lives, violence against civilians, mass displacement and migration and continue to unfold as an acute humanitarian crisis;

and whereas the Stateless Rohingya people have been subjected to inhuman and cruel treatment at the hands of various forces resulting in a catastrophic humanitarian crisis;

and whereas the international community has called for the immediate halt to violence and the restoration of law and order and protection of life and property of people of conflict areas;

This Motion urges the Government as a matter of urgency to call on the Government of Myanmar to take all measures necessary to end the violence and protect people from atrocities and commence a dialogue with all stakeholders with a view to arriving at a lasting and acceptable solution to the Rohingya issue.тАЭ

Sir, I submitted this Motion at the request of my Party Leader, the Hon. Rauff Hakeem, the Minister of City Planning and Water Supply. He was due to speak but unfortunately, he had to leave the Chamber due to a personal matter. So, I may make a little contribution to the Debate by way of an explanation.

There are about a million or more Rohingya in Myanmar today of whom 80 per cent live in Rakhine State. It is generally believed in Myanmar that Rohingya migrated to Rakhine State during and after the British colonial era. However, most experts outside Myanmar agree that the Rohingya have been living in Rakhine State since at least the 15th century, and possibly as early as the 7th century.

Rakhine was a Kingdom from ancient times and was known as Arakaan. Rakhine came under Burmese control in 1784. Subsequently it was incorporated to British India consequent to the first Anglo-Burmese War between 1824-1826 and Burma became a British colony in 1885. Finally Burma attained Independence in 1948.

Myanmar is one of the most ethnically diverse countries in the world with 135 officially recognized races, but Rohingya is not recognized as one. Almost every ethnic group in Burma has rebelled during the countryтАЩs history and some of them continue to do so. It is believed interracial tension was a result of the colonial past.

553 554

[р╢ЬL р╢Ьр╖П7├Т р╢вр╢║┬кр╢╕ р╖Щр╢┤р╖Щ&р╢╗р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П]

2017 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& 21

Just before gaining Independence in 1947, the Burmese Government and a number of recognized ethnic groups signed the Panglong Agreement with a view to solve longstanding demands of various ethnic groups.

The second round of the Union Peace Conference, called, "the 21st Century Panglong Conference," was held in May, this year. This time too Rohingya was not invited.

Many claim that the unfolding situation in the Rakhine State is exaggerated and blown out of proportion for propaganda. Further, it was claimed that Rohingya is not persecuted or discriminated against. But the fact remains that Rohingya is stateless even today and subject to most inhuman treatment at the hands of various forces.

I would pose the question with respect that, if Rohingya issue is not serious, one failed to understand why an Advisory Commission on Rakhine State was appointed in September, 2016 at the request of Aung San Suu Kyi. The Commission chaired by ex-Secretary General of UN, Mr. Kofi Annan is mandated to analyse the present situation of all communities in Rakhine State.

There have been a number of cycles of violence against Rohingya from time to time. Every time lives were lost, there was mass displacement and persecution of people. The current wave of violence has resulted in more than 400,000 Rohingya fleeing Myanmar of which half of them are children. According to witness and mass media reports after Rohingya flee, their homes, the entire villages and their belongings were being destroyed totally erasing any evidence of human habitation. This has all the hallmarks of ethnic cleansing. In fact, the UN Secretary-General Antonio Guterres has branded it as a тАЬtextbook example of ethnic cleansing.тАЭ He said at a recent press meet, тАЬWhen one-third of the Rohingya population had to flee the country, could you find a better word to describe it?тАЭ It is unfortunate that these unprecedented human rights violations and crimes against humanity take place after the transition of Myanmar to civilian rule under the leadership of Nobel laureate Aung San Suu Kyi.

The global community has a moral responsibility and right to seek justice of Rohingya people. Responsibility to protect is a global political commitment which was endorsed by all member states of the United Nations at the 2005 World Summit to prevent genocide, war crimes, ethnic cleansing and crimes against humanity.

Sri Lanka offers a unique example of solving issues relating to stateless people through legal and diplomatic initiatives. In fact, the Second Republican Constitution specially protected the stateless persons through grant of certain Fundamental Rights to them.

Sri Lanka and Myanmar have been close allies and friends for almost seven decades. Diplomatic relations with Myanmar commenced in 1949 and our Mission in Yangon was one of the first five overseas Missions opened by Sri Lanka after Independence.

Even before commencing modern day formal diplomatic relations, Theravada Buddhism was the link

between the two countries. There have been frequent exchanges of pilgrims and scriptural knowledge. Origins of Ramanna and Amarapura Nikayas can be traced to Burmese influence and assistance.

Kings of Sri Lanka especially Vijayabahu I, who was in conflict with Cholas, received economic aid from King Anawrahta of Burma and also received assistance in re-organizing the sangha in Sri Lanka. Therefore, both the countries have many things in common.

In this context, I would urge the Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs and the Government to use the friendship and cordial relationship with Myanmar and urge the Government of Myanmar to protect Rohingya people and also enter into a dialogue with the parties concerned.

I thank you. р╢Ь. Zр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П[р╢к р╢╕┬в-р╢╕р╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ родрпИро▓рпИроородро╛0 роЙ,.рокро┐рой роЕро╡роХ ) (The Hon. Presiding Member) р╖Щр╢║р╢вр╢▒р╖Пр╖А р╖Гр╖Кiр╢╗ "#р╢╕, р╢ЬL g├Рz& р╢╗┬Шр╢╕р╖П' р╢╕'S р╢╕р╖П. [р╢Е.р╢╖р╖П. 6.25] р╢Ь. qwo р╢╗┬бр╢╕р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ роЬро┐  ро░ро╣рпБрооро╛) (The Hon. р╢Ь. Zр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П[р╢к р╢╕┬в-р╢╕р╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ родрпИро▓рпИроородро╛0 роЙ,.рокро┐рой роЕро╡роХ ) (The Hon. Tilak Marapana) р╢ФH. р╢Ь. Zр╢╜р╖Пр╖Гр╢▒р╖П[р╢к р╢╕┬в-р╢╕р╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ родрпИро▓рпИроородро╛0 роЙ,.рокро┐рой роЕро╡роХ ) (The Hon. Presiding Member) р╢ЬL р╢Зр╢╕? р╢╕р╖Пр╢з р╢║'р╢▒ ?р╖Щр╢╢р╢▒ Nр╖Гр╖П, р╢пр╖Р' р╢С р╢╕р╖П р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╢╗р╢▒р╖Ар╖П. р╢Кр╢з р╢┤┬бр╖А р╢Ер╖Щр╢▒sM р╢ЬL р╢╕'Sр╖АL'р╢з р╢Ър╢ор╖П р╢Ър╢╗'р╢▒ р╖А'. [6.37p.m.] р╢Ь. р╢╜" р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╢┤р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (р╖Гр╢Вр╖Ар╢░р╢▒ р╢Ър╖Пр╢║р╢╖р╖Пр╢╗ р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нe-р╢╕р╖П р╖Гр╖Д Iр╖Щ1р╖Б р╢Ър╢з@- р╢Ер╢╕р╖Пр╢нe-р╢╕р╖П) (рооро╛ рооро┐ родро┐ро▓ рооро╛ро░рокрой - роЕрокро┐ро╡ро┐ 'родро┐. рокрогро┐. рпЖрокро╛,. роХ роЕрпИроо/роЪ  рпЖро╡ро│ро┐роиро╛1роЯAро╡8роХ роЕрпИроо/роЪ ) (The Hon. Tilak Marapana -Minister of Development Assignments and Minister of Foreign Affairs) Hon. Presiding Member, the Rohingya issue is very complicated and has a very long history. But, the issue has attracted global attention after the violence that took place in the State of Rakhine.

We know that close to one million Rakhaines had fled to Bangladesh and to other neighbouring countries as refugees. International attention is drawn to this issue as day by day, the situation is worsening due to lack of food, shelter, health facilities and environmental reasons. Likewise, the Government of Sri Lanka is concerned about the humanitarian aspect of the refugees and the emerging tension between Bangladesh and Myanmar, both friendly countries of Sri Lanka.

Sri Lanka is closely studying the statements issued by the UN, the UN High Commissioner for Refugees - UNHCR - the UN Human Rights Council, rights groups and countries that are concerned on the issue.

Sir, Sri Lanka and Myanmar are steeped in history based on Theravada Buddhism. Our relations date back to the Fourth Century BC, where monks from Myanmar frequently visited the Mahavihara of Anuradhapura to imbibe orthodox traditions of Buddhism in order to propagate those in their own country. In 1865, with the establishment of the Ramanna Nikaya, it was an unparalleled milestone of the relations between both countries. Sri Lanka and Myanmar have been enjoying good relations in multifaceted areas of cooperation, which have consolidated further with the establishment of diplomatic relations in 1949. I say these things because then, you may agree that the issue is very sensitive to the Buddhists in Sri Lanka and also we have to look at the concerns of the Muslims of Sri Lanka. Therefore, Sri Lanka should have a rational and a cautious approach to this issue.

559 560

р╢┤р╖П&Dр╖Щ.' р╖А

The Government of Sri Lanka has continued to closely observe the situation with regard to the Rohingya community and to cooperate with the international and regional initiatives in addressing the issue of the Rohingya community. Despite not being a signatory to the 1951 Convention and the 1967 Protocol on the Status of Refugees, Sri Lanka has been handling cases of asylum seekers or refugees in terms of the Agreement signed between the Government of Sri Lanka and the UNHCR in 2005.

I might add here that even Rohingya refugees have been given shelter in Sri Lanka in the past. If there are any refugees that spill over, we will, on humanitarian grounds, not look the other way but render whatever assistance we can to those persons.

Sri Lanka is deeply concerned over the current developments in the Rakhine State that has drawn the attention of the international community. The Government of Sri Lanka calls on the Government of Myanmar to take urgent measures to ensure the safety and security of all civilians in the region and bring the law and order situation under control. Sri Lanka firmly believes that Myanmar as a close friend of Sri Lanka, will win the credibility of the international community by restoring law and order, peace and stability through legitimate means.

Thank you, Presiding Member. [6.41p.m.] р╢Ь. р╖Щр╖ГLlE р╢Е┬Р р╖Гр╖П┬С р╢╕~р╢╜р╖Пр╢▒р╖П р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П (рооро╛ рооро┐ рпЖроЪропро┐1 роЕ; ро╕ро╛ро╣ро┐ рпЖроорпЧро▓ро╛ройро╛ ) (The Hon. Seyed Ali Zahir Moulana ) Hon. Presiding Member, I take this opportunity to draw the attention of this House to the plight of Rohingya people in the Rakhine Province of Myanmar.

This is a very sad occasion. It is sad because the situation that we speak about betrays our trust in a country, which all believed was returning to democracy, rule of law and human rights after several years of international isolation and instability.

Having listened to the Foreign Minister, our concern today is not intended to criticize the country and its people, nor do we seek to blame a religion or language. Because we do not believe that the country or its religion or religions could be blamed for what carnage an extremist segment is causing, supported or condoned by some in power. Hon. Presiding Member, on the contrary, our remarks today are a reflection of a deep sense of disappointment or frustration at the continuing streak of violence of a genocidal proportions or ethnic cleansing in a particular country.

We in Sri Lanka can easily comprehend the roots of the crisis in Myanmar. Colonial history has shaped the conflict after the emergence of the independent nation

State of Myanmar, just as colonial rule created dissension and conflict among communities during our kings of yore.

The Rohingya people are today described as "stateless" by their Government. To the majority community they are unwanted intruders and a threat to their nation-State. They think they are an inconvenience to their overarching national identity. Today, they have become the world's most conspicuous people, homeless in their own land and adrift in the waters of the Bay of Bengal.

Hon. Presiding Member, not a single day passes without the international media as well as the human rights community reporting on the horrendous crimes being committed against the people of the Rakhine Province of Myanmar. The unfortunate plight of these Rohingya people has been starting squarely in the face of humanity for a few years now, with its intensity at unprecedented levels in the last few weeks.

When crimes against humanity are perpetrated against a people on the grounds of race, religion, language, ethnicity or on any other discriminative reasons, which appear repugnant to human conscience, it is our collective duty to do all that is within our power to help bring an immediate end to it, ensure amelioration of the conditions of persecuted people, and to work with partners in the region and the world to facilitate their peaceful living including return and resettlement in safety and dignity with guarantees of protection and non-recurrence in the future. It is our strong belief that Sri Lanka, under the National Unity Government, is in a position to demonstrate initiative and/or to give a leadership in ensuring such a positive outcome through peaceful means.

Therefore, I would like to propose the Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs to adopt the following measures to resolve this terrible calamity that has overtaken the people of Myanmar who are regarded as people known for their tranquil temperament and sedate lifestyle of a pious Buddhist social order:

The Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs should summon the Ambassador of Myanmar based in Colombo to share our concerns with the Government of Myanmar, urging an immediate end to violence against the Rohingya people in the interest of peace and stability in the region;

We should offer relief and rehabilitation assistance to the affected people through credible international agencies;

Sri Lanka should issue a public statement demonstrating its clear interest in addressing the situation faced by the Rohingya people and ensuring peace and stability in the region; and

Call a Debate or Session in Parliament to explain the position of the Government of Sri Lanka urging for non-violence and peace building in the Rakhine Province of Myanmar.

561 562

[р╢ЬL ?р╢╜ р╢╕р╖Пр╢╗р╢┤р╢▒ р╢╕р╖Др╢нр╖П]

2017 р╖Гр╖Р=р╢нр╖Р.р╢╢& 21

The Government of Sri Lanka is well-placed to undertake all of these measures as we ourselves are today embarked on the path of reconciliation and peace-building. Sri Lanka is committed to the pursuit of peace and stability in the region which remains critical to the realization of its vision of a harmonious, inclusive and sustainable Indian Ocean, as part of its Vision 2025. We would encourage the Government of Sri Lanka, the Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to initiate urgent appropriate measures and clearly demonstrate our commitment and leadership.

Thank you. [рокро┐.рок. 6.48]

Parliament adjourned accordingly at 6.57p.m. until 10.30 a.m. on Friday, 22nd September, 2017, pursuant to the Resolution of Parliament of 08th March, 2016.
